   nirargalarasāsāragarbhasandarbhasaṃpadā pratipadaṃ prativākyaṃ	nirargala rasa AsAra garBa sandarBa saMpadA pratipadam prativAkyam
   pratiprakaraṇaṃ ca prakāśamānābhinavabhaṅgīprāyāḥ bhrājiṣṇavo	pratiprakaraNam ca prakASamAna aBinava BaFgI prAyAH BrAjizNavaH 
   navonabonmīlitanāyakādbhutaguṇotkarṣākarṣāḥ harṣātirekamanekaśo	navonaba unmIlita nAyaka adButa guNa utkarza AkarzAH harza atirekam anekaSas 
   'pyāsvādyamānāḥ samutpādayanti sahṛdayānām /	api AsvAdyamAnAH samutpAdayanti sahRdayAnAm /
   evamanyadapi nidarśanāntaramudbhāvanīyam /	evam anyat api nidarSana antaram udBAvanIyam /
   kathonmeṣe samāne 'pi vapuṣīva nijairguṇaiḥ /	kaTA unmeze samAne api vapuzi iva nijEH guNEH /

   ityantaraślokaḥ /	iti antaraSlokaH /
   bhūyo 'pyasyā bhedamupapādayati   	BUyas api asyAH Bedam upapAdayati   
   mahākaviprabandhānāṃ sarveṣāmasti vakratā /	mahAkavi prabanDAnAm sarvezAm asti vakra tA /
   nūtanopāyaniṣpannanayavartmopadeśinām // Vjiv_4.26 //	nUtana upAya nizpanna naya vartma upadeSinAm // Vjiu _4.26 //
   "mahākaviprabandhanām"   navanirmāṇanipuṇanirupamakaviprakāṇḍa	"mahAkavi prabanDa nAm"   nava nirmANa nipuNa nirupamaka viprakANxa
   (viracitānāṃ) "sarveṣāṃ" /	(viracitAnAn) "sarvezAn" /
   (kiṃbhūtānāṃ)  "nūtanopāyaniṣapannanayavartmo	(kiMBUtAnAM)  "nUtana upAya nizapan= a naya vartmaH 
   padeśināṃ"   "nūtanāḥ"   pratyagrāḥ, "upāyāḥ"   sāmādiprayogaprakārāḥ	padeSinA aM"   "nUtanAH"    pratyagrAH, "upAyAH "    sAma Adi prayoga prakArAH
   tadvidāṃ gocarā ye "tairniṣpannaṃ' siddhaṃ yat "nayavartma" nīti (mārgaḥ)	tad vidAm gocarAH ye "tEH nizpannama sidDam yat "naya vartma" nIti (mArgaH)
   tadupadiśanti śikṣayanti ye (te) tathoktāsteṣām /	tat upadiSanti Sikzayanti ye (te) taTA uktAH tezAm /
   kimuktaṃ bhavati   sakaleṣvapi satkaviprabandhaṣu	kim uktam Bavati    sakalezu api sat kavi prabanDazu
   abhinavabhaṅgīniveśapeśalinyā nītyāḥ phalamupapadyamānaṃ	aBinava BaFgI niveSa peSalinyAH nItyAH Palam upapadyamAnam
   pratipādyopadeśadvāreṇa kimapi camatkāraṇamupalabhyata eva /	pratipAdya upadeSa dvAreNa kim api camat kAraNam upalaByate eva /
   yathā mudrārākṣase    tatra hi	yaTA mudrA rAkzase   tatra hi
   pravaraprajñāprabhāvaprapañcitavicitranītivyāpārāḥ pragalbhanta eva /	pravara prajQA praBAva prapaQcita vicitra nIti vyApArAH pragalBante eva /
   yathā ca tāpasavatsarājoddeśa eva vyākhyātaḥ /	yaTA ca tApasa vat sa rAja uddeSaH eva vyAKyAtaH /
   evamanyadapyutprekṣaṇīyam /	evam anyat api utprekzaNIyam /
